Current Affairs Commentary

How to Defend the Sui Frontier 44

— Li

Since the bandit raids by Mongolian bandits that repeatedly harassed the Sui border were repelled by Fu Zuoyi's troops, the situation within Suiyuan seemed calm for a while. However, historical experience tells us that quiet during great turmoil is often a prelude to further deterioration. Indeed, the situation in Suiyuan has recently become tense again with the large-scale military exercises by Japanese troops in Peiping and Tianjin. The puppet army of Li Shouxin, instigated by a certain party, has advanced to Shangdu, urging Wang Ying's cavalry bandits to move westward. Skirmishes have already occurred between patrols near Taolin and Horinger. At the same time, a large batch of military supplies provided by a certain party has been transported to Shangdu. Aircraft from a certain party frequently conduct reconnaissance in the skies over eastern Suiyuan. The formal start of war is probably only a matter of time.

Suiyuan has now become the front line of national defense, and its position is, needless to say, extremely important. The Peiping-Suiyuan Railway, which runs across the territory, connects closely from Baotou, through Guihua, Jining, Datong, and Zhangjiakou, to Peiping and the transportation network within the Great Wall. The northern side of the railway is dominated by the Daqing Mountains, forming the Suiyuan Northeast Plateau, which also has a very important strategic position. The current confrontation between the puppet army and General Fu Zuoyi's troops is along the Daqing Mountains and the border of Chahar and Suiyuan in eastern Suiyuan. This is the gateway to Suiyuan. If it is not defended, not only will the entire province of Suiyuan be difficult to protect, but also Hebei, Chahar, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, and Outer Mongolia will feel a great threat.

Everyone knows that the puppet army's invasion of Suiyuan is a plan long decided by a certain party. If a certain party uses the puppet army to occupy Suiyuan, on the one hand, it can advance southwest, invade Shanxi and Shaanxi, control the Tongpu and Zhengtai Railways, and complete the military encirclement of the five provinces of North China, crossing the Yellow River to threaten Xi'an and disturb the central cities of the Northwest. On the other hand, it can advance westward, invade Ningxia, cross the Helan Mountains, pass through Alxa League, and reach Xinjiang to encircle Outer Mongolia. Therefore, the survival of Suiyuan is really related to the survival of all of China. We can easily understand this from a certain party's continental policy.

We must do our utmost to maintain the integrity of national territory and sovereignty, especially since Suiyuan is the gateway to North and Northwest China. Now, General Fu Zuoyi, who is stationed in Suiyuan, has repeatedly declared his determination to defend the country to the death. If the enemy dares to invade Suiyuan, he will lead his brave soldiers to inflict a heavy blow. This sincere expression of defending the country is very admirable. However, since the enemy has a far-reaching plan to invade Suiyuan, we must make more thorough preparations. Generally speaking, the government must do its utmost to strengthen the forces of the Suiyuan defense army, and the people must be determined to provide General Fu Zuoyi and others with all kinds of powerful assistance. This has become our current necessary obligation.

Eager Expectations from All Sides: Roosevelt to Unfold New Plans, Promoting World Peace After Internal Stabilization, Completing Recovery Through Trade Development 45

(Washington) Roosevelt's re-election as president by an overwhelming majority is tantamount to the American people giving him a completely blank check to fill in as he pleases. No president in American history has ever been granted such great power. During the election campaign, Roosevelt only made general statements on his political platform. He made no promises on the National Recovery Administration, the Agricultural Adjustment Administration, the Supreme Court, or the Constitution. In the future, he can freely propose plans that he deems appropriate. Although it is extremely unlikely that the United States will join the World Court and the League of Nations, the president has not said a word to reassure people on this point. Although his new administrative plan has not yet been revealed, according to informed sources, the president's policy in his second term will focus on consolidating the foundations laid in his first term. Once the president expresses satisfaction with the tranquility of domestic affairs, he will use his increased prestige and power to work towards stabilizing the troubled world. He will first convene a peace conference in the capital of Argentina, and Secretary of State Hull will attend this meeting. Rumors suggest that Roosevelt intends to personally attend, but this has not been confirmed. It is generally believed that the president's official duties are too heavy, making it difficult for him to leave Washington for a month. The president sincerely hopes that this conference will achieve a satisfactory conclusion, because if Roosevelt can complete the unification of the Americas and create a peaceful Western Hemisphere, then his opportunity to attract the world to listen to his call for peace will increase. The president has a strong will and is unlikely to harbor any illusions of President Wilson. However, the mandate for peace and reconstruction that President Wilson received in the past cannot be compared with the mandate that Roosevelt has just received. Moreover, Roosevelt is a great idealist, so the future remains to be seen. Father Coughlin, a radio propagandist who supported the Union Party candidate Landon, commented on President Roosevelt's victory today, saying that future historians will spend less time studying Caesar and Napoleon and more time studying Roosevelt. Roosevelt can easily become a dictator. The power he holds is greater than that of any figure in history. The so-called minority is now purely a theoretical term. Smith, a famous Democrat who opposed Roosevelt in this election, also told guests that the people of the whole country have expressed their common will. The main principle of democracy is the advocacy of the majority of the people. Every citizen and every true American must now fully support President Roosevelt. Secretary of State Hull said that the results of this election prove that the United States' efforts to promote peace and its insistence on strict neutrality during wartime are more effective. Hull also guaranteed that this policy will continue as before. (Reuters, 5th)

(New York) According to general observers, Roosevelt's majority in this election is much larger than in 1932. This result will have a significant impact on domestic and foreign affairs. In terms of domestic affairs, some of Roosevelt's economic policies have been ruled unconstitutional by the Supreme Court. Now that the election results have proven that the people have increased confidence in the president, Roosevelt's economic policies will naturally be further strengthened in the future. Regarding foreign affairs, given the current situation in Europe, the president will also adopt a bolder policy to deal with it. Some people even believe that the president may amend the current Neutrality Act so that the ban on the export of military supplies will no longer be uniformly applied to belligerent countries, without distinguishing between aggressor and victim. (Havas, 4th)

(Washington) State Department officials announced today that the Democratic Party's overwhelming victory in the election has enabled Secretary of State Hull to intensify the implementation of trade development plans in order to seek economic recovery, thereby consolidating world peace and promoting human happiness. Trade development is beneficial to the United States and other countries. Roosevelt's re-election is a guarantee that tariffs will not be raised again. After the Inter-American Conference for the Maintenance of Peace convenes in the capital of Argentina in January next year, many new trade agreements can be established. Hull intends to submit a Western Hemisphere peace plan to the conference as a model for world peace. Other responsible persons said that the United States will likely continue to build a navy to effectively rival Britain. This navy will probably still be concentrated in the Pacific to prevent the outbreak of war in the Far East. However, if American interests in the Far East are not infringed, it will probably continue to adopt a policy of compromise towards China and Japan. The president will probably be more conservative on monetary issues in the future, but if it can help stabilize international currencies and promote world trade, the president is also willing to support it. (National Telegram, 4th)

Roosevelt's Declaration: Advancing Together with the People; Landon's Governorship Also Not Guaranteed, to Return to Old Business of Oil and Gas 46

Hyde Park. President Roosevelt received congratulatory letters and telegrams from all sides at home today like snowflakes, saying that the people's great trust proves that we are now advancing together, and his heart is filled with joy. It is believed that President Roosevelt will give the country a breathing opportunity before Congress convenes in January next year. (National Telegram, 5th)

Topeka. Republican presidential candidate Landon laughed off his election defeat and went to the governor's office today to sort out documents in preparation for the handover in January next year. It is learned that after Landon gets rid of his governorship of Kansas, he will return to his old business of oil and gas. (National Telegram, 4th)

(New York) Political figures recently declared that the ministers of various departments will be changed one after another after January 1 next year. At that time, Postmaster General Farley will abandon his political career, and Secretary of Commerce Roper, Secretary of the Navy Swanson, Acting Secretary of War Woodring, Secretary of Labor Perkins, and Attorney General Cummings will also retire successively. Among them, it is said that the position of Secretary of Commerce may be filled by Mayor La Guardia of New York. (Havas, 5th)

(New York) The Democratic Party's great victory in this election will cause three famous American figures to be cast off the political stage. One is Landon, the Republican candidate who failed in this election, whose governorship of Kansas has been taken by Democrat Huxman. One is former President Hoover, and the other is Smith. Smith was originally a member of the Democratic Party, but suddenly opposed Roosevelt in this election. Twenty-seven Democratic members and six Republican members have been elected as governors. Murphy, the American Commissioner to the Philippines, is currently on leave in the United States and has now been elected as the governor of Michigan. (Reuters, 4th)

(New York) President Roosevelt's unprecedented victory has fundamentally shaken the party structure. According to the reorganization movement of American political parties, since 1912, there have been signs. In the next four years, it seems that there will be historical progress. Pennsylvania has always been the Republican Party's base camp, but this time it has completely changed and has no power. The same is true for the New England states. However, observers carefully examine the inside of the Democratic Party and see significant cracks. Conservatives such as Senators Glass and Byrd may unite with Smith and others who opposed Roosevelt this time to seek control of the government. Moreover, the more conservative members in the South will also find it difficult to agree with the radical elements in the North for a long time. Therefore, by 1940, there will inevitably be serious disputes within the Democratic Party. However, observers also believe that Roosevelt will take advantage of the opportunity of this majority of the people's trust to carry out his administrative policies without compromising with conservative elements. (National Telegram, 4th)

President Roosevelt to Visit the Philippines 47

Detroit. American High Commissioner to the Philippines Murphy, after being elected as Governor of Michigan, told reporters from the Associated Press today that President Roosevelt may visit the Philippines during his second term. If the president makes the trip, he will try to follow along. He also said that he will continue to perform his duties as commissioner here until he takes office as governor next January. The rumor that Murphy will be appointed as Secretary of War has been denied by Murphy today. (National Telegram, 5th)

(Washington) According to reliable sources today, although American High Commissioner to the Philippines Murphy has been elected as Governor of Michigan, he will continue to be President Roosevelt's closest advisor on Philippine affairs in the future, and will also pay close attention to the preparatory talks for the economic conference to be held next year. Regarding the island's political situation, it is believed today that Roosevelt's re-election as president is very beneficial to the Philippines, because the economic relations between the two countries will not be changed, and Roosevelt is the most qualified to solve the issue of the United States maintaining a naval base in the Philippines. Secretary of State Hull's foreign policy has always advocated stability in the Pacific, and Vice President Garner has more influence over the United States' Philippine policy. Therefore, the results of this election have made it impossible for the Republican Party to advocate immediate independence for the Philippines or to increase trade barriers between the United States and the Philippines. (National Telegram, 5th)

Election Results 48

(New York) The 531 electoral representatives from the 48 states across the country were all elected before midnight the day before yesterday. As of 3:00 a.m. this morning, the vote counting results from each state showed that the Democratic Party had won in 46 states, with a total of 23,822,442 votes. The electoral representatives thus elected totaled 523. The Republican Party won only in Maine and Vermont, with a total of 14,835,381 votes. The electoral representatives thus elected were only eight. (Havas, 5th)

(New York) As of the time of this dispatch, the number of votes won by the Democratic Party in the re-election of the Senate and House of Representatives has also increased. Of the 435 members of the House of Representatives, the Democratic Party already has 316 members, the Republican Party only has 87 members, the Progressive Party has 6 members, and the Labor Party has 3 members. It is not yet known which party the remaining 23 seats belong to. (Note: In the previous House of Representatives, there were 313 Democrats, 117 Republicans, and 5 Labor Party members.) Of the 96 senators, the Democratic Party already has 71 members (including 47 who were not re-elected), the Republican Party has 17 members, the Labor Party has 2 members, and the Progressive Party has 1 member. It is not yet known which party the remaining 5 members belong to. (Note: In the previous Senate, there were 59 Democrats, 36 Republicans, and 1 Labor Party member.) (Havas, 5th)

(New York) President Roosevelt's election victory has given the ruling party an unprecedented majority in the House of Representatives. The Democratic Party's candidate for member of the House of Representatives won a total of 339 seats, an increase of seven seats compared to 1934. The Republican Party has decreased from 103 seats to 85 seats. However, the national vote count has not yet been completely revealed, so the final result may be slightly changed. In the Senate, the Democratic Party occupies 74 seats, which is also an unprecedented record. The Republican Party only won 18 seats. (National Telegram, 4th)

(New York) After this election, the Democratic Party has an absolute majority in both the Senate and the House of Representatives. The new House of Representatives has five female members, one less than the previous session. Those who were re-elected are Ms. Norton, Ms. Wold, and Ms. Jenckes, all of whom belong to the Democratic Party. In addition, Ms. Rogers belongs to the Republican Party. The newly elected women are Democrat Ms. Halleck and Republican Ms. Kahn. Ms. Kahn, who had been a member of the House of Representatives for 12 years, was defeated this time. Also, Democrat Ms. Greenway was not re-elected. (Reuters, 4th)

(New York) Five senators who strongly opposed the New Deal have been defeated by the Democrats. Their names are as follows: Hastings of Delaware, Carey of Wyoming, Metcalf of Rhode Island, Dickinson of Iowa, and Barbour of New Jersey. The Republican Party now has only 18 seats in the Senate. (National Society Telegram, 4th)

Our Country Expresses Gratification at President Roosevelt's Re-election; Will Use Full Strength to Seek World Peace Hereafter 49

(Nanjing) The preliminary results of the U.S. presidential election have now made it clear that the incumbent President Roosevelt has obtained an absolute majority of electoral votes. There is no doubt that he will be elected in the second election on December 10. After this news came, the people of our country expressed gratification. According to those familiar with international politics, Roosevelt is heroic and promising, not only an outstanding president of the United States, but also one of the great politicians of the modern world. Since taking office in 1933, he resolutely implemented the New Deal to restore economic prosperity. Although his achievements are still pending, domestic reforms are gradually being completed. In the next four years, he will be able to use his full strength, with a resolute and active attitude, to seek world peace and stability in East Asia, which we rely on. We will wait and see. (Central News Agency Telegram, 5th)

European Reactions 50

(London) The great victory of U.S. President Roosevelt in the election has greatly surprised Germany, while Italy and France are quite pleased. German newspapers commented that the democratic countries of the world are now concentrating certain election votes, hoping that this move can change the face of the world. Italy recalled Roosevelt's non-participation in sanctions against Italy, praising Roosevelt as the most fascist-style politician in the United States. French Foreign Minister Delbos said that France is extremely pleased with Roosevelt's unprecedented victory, and said that this move can enable Roosevelt to make greater efforts to become the avant-garde of culture. Roosevelt's re-election can make the success of French-American doctrine more possible. (Reuters, 5th)

(London) People here are calm as usual about President Roosevelt's re-election, only showing slight surprise at the number of votes Roosevelt received. The gold and silver exchanges are quite optimistic about the future of silver prices, because Roosevelt may continue to pursue the silver purchase policy. However, another group of people said that Roosevelt himself does not fully support this policy, and even if it is still adopted in the future, it will probably be subject to considerable modification. (Reuters, 4th)

Price Increases 51

(New York) Mr. Naller, the president of the Price Research Association, spoke to reporters from the Associated Press today, predicting that after President Roosevelt's re-election, prices in the United States will generally rise, with sugar prices being particularly high, because sugar prices depend entirely on Jones' Sugar Import Act for their transfer. Now that Roosevelt has been elected, the act will not change, so sugar prices will rise significantly. (National Telegram, 4th)

(New York) The most attention on Wall Street is the tax law on undistributed profits and what the repercussions will be, because since the Democratic Party's election victory, there is no hope of abolishing this tax law. It is now believed that dividends will increase, and all outstanding interest on preferred stocks will be cleared. The prices of most stocks have risen. Wall Street is quite calm about Roosevelt's re-election. It is estimated that the total amount of money bet on Roosevelt's victory on election day reached 5 million yuan, with a ratio of seven to two. (Reuters, 5th)

(Tokyo) The Navy's regular personnel transfer order for this year will be issued on December 1. It is reported that Admiral Takahashi, the current Commander of the Combined Fleet, will be transferred to the position of Military Councilor, and Vice Admiral Mitsumasa Yonai, the Commander of the Yokosuka Naval District, will be promoted to Commander of the Combined Fleet. (Allied Press Telegram, 5th)

Two Commit Suicide in Protest of the American Republican Party's Failure 53

(New York) Two people here actually committed suicide in anger because of the Republican Party's election failure. The owner of a coffee shop in Kansas City had told his wife the other day that if Republican presidential candidate Landon failed, he would commit suicide. Later, when he saw that the Democratic Party had indeed won, he shot himself to death with a pistol. Also, one person in a meeting place in Randolph, Vermont, quietly left the venue after hearing that the Democratic Party had won a great victory and Roosevelt had been re-elected. Afterward, friends discovered that he had shot himself at home. (Reuters, 5th)

Spanish Rebel Army Shells the Southern Suburbs of the Western Capital; Outpost Only Three Miles from the Capital; Government Troops' Two Counterattacks Fail; A Call for All Able-Bodied Men to Go to the Front Lines 54

Lisbon: Spanish Nationalist forces today began shelling the southern suburbs of Madrid. Assault troops are awaiting orders to attack the city. (National Telegram, 4th)

Madrid: Rebel forces began bombing the capital city at 9:20 PM tonight. Government troops are busy deploying cannons and tanks around the city in preparation for a final battle. The sound of shelling is clearly audible in the capital. Several rebel aircraft continue to bomb the city's surrounding defenses. Two planes flew directly over the capital at noon but were driven back by government anti-aircraft fire. (National Telegram, 4th)

Madrid: The sound of shelling can be heard in the suburbs. Small units of Nationalist troops have even advanced to encamp near the city. The government has published a message to the public in newspapers, stating that rebel forces are pressing in, and "All our citizens must be prepared for battle at any moment. It is victory or death." The government has also implemented a city-wide blackout to strengthen defenses. All lights must be turned off from 10:00 PM each day. Except for militia patrolling the streets with weapons, no one is allowed to pass through. Furthermore, preparations are being made for a general mobilization order. All streets are pitch black at night, but the rumble of trucks can be heard, presumably transporting reinforcements to the front lines. Residents remain calm and show no signs of panic. Thousands of citizens are building defenses and obstacles in and around the city. (Havas Telegram, 5th)

Seville: Nationalist forces have advanced to the town of Carabanchel, three miles from Getafe airfield and about three miles from the center of Madrid. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

Madrid: Since the fall of Getafe airfield, the defenses of Madrid have been further strengthened. The paving stones of the city's major roads have been completely dug up to build obstacles. These construction works are carried out by elderly men and women, assisted by children who load soil into baskets for the elderly to use. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

Lisbon: After the Spanish Nationalist forces occupied the Getafe airfield, only nine miles from Madrid, last night, the fall of Madrid became imminent. When Nationalist General Varela personally led his troops to the town, he told news reporters, "You can inform the world that Madrid will be occupied by the Nationalist forces this week." The general also said that according to Nationalist aircraft reports, the road from Madrid to Valencia is blocked by thousands of refugees fleeing the endangered capital. In Burgos, preparations are underway to celebrate the Nationalist forces' capture of Madrid. Local Catholic churches are also preparing sacred artifacts to hold a Holy Communion to celebrate the victory. The fall of Getafe followed five hours of fierce fighting, with both sides using tanks and aircraft. The Moroccan troops finally launched a brave bayonet charge, and the government militia abandoned six tanks and retreated. The entire town has now been reduced to ashes. The Nationalist forces claim that a Russian general and two Spanish generals attempted to prevent the militia from retreating but ultimately failed. As a result of yesterday's fierce fighting, the Nationalist forces repelled the elite Asturian miners, making the Nationalist forces the masters of all of Galicia. Over a hundred miners died in yesterday's battle, abandoning several boxes of hand grenades. There was also fighting on the road from Gijón to Oviedo, with many supporters of the government killed. As a result, the government militia retreated to the town of Santander. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

Getafe: Two columns of Nationalist forces on the south side of the capital, one led by Lieutenant Colonel De la Puente, departing from Fuenlabrada, and the other led by Colonel Barron, departing from the village of Parla, engaged in fierce fighting with government troops. By 2:15 PM, they had defeated the government troops and stormed into the town of Getafe. By this time, the main force of the government troops had already retreated, leaving only a few hundred militiamen ambushed in some houses in the town, continuing to open fire to provide cover. At 2:30 PM, the airfield's oil depot in the town was hit by a shell and caught fire, with thick smoke rising. Half an hour later, the last batch of militiamen also completely withdrew. The town of Getafe was then under the control of the Nationalist forces. More than a dozen militiamen surrendered to the Nationalist forces and told our reporter that they had arrived in Getafe from the capital three days ago. Several members of the revolutionary committee in the capital are only engaged in looting residents, and food is extremely scarce, with only militiamen receiving the necessary food. (Havas Telegram, 4th)

Parla: A special dispatch from our reporter states that after fierce fighting on the south side of the capital yesterday, the Nationalist forces not only occupied the town of Getafe (13 kilometers south of Madrid, the location of the government's airfield), but also occupied the towns of Leganés and Alcorcón, which are suburbs of Madrid. Although government troops were dispatched from the towns of Torrelodones and Villaviciosa de Odón in an attempt to counterattack, they were all repelled. The main force of the Nationalist army, commanded by General Varela, commander of the central route, is no more than 15 kilometers from the capital. The government troops defending the "Cuatro Vientos" airfield have now withdrawn. The original 14 aircraft in the airfield have also flown away. Fires have broken out around Madrid, and thick smoke is rising, as if shrouded in dark clouds. It is expected that the Nationalist forces will soon advance on the capital. (Havas Telegram, 5th)

Ávila: A special dispatch from our reporter states that the Nationalist forces defeated government troops near the village of Villaviciosa de Odón, south of the capital, yesterday and occupied the village. On the government side, 5,000 militiamen and 30 tanks participated in the battle, but after two hours of fierce fighting, they were defeated, with 400 killed and four tanks abandoned. Another three were destroyed by the Nationalist forces. The Nationalist forces' outpost there is now only seven kilometers from Madrid. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

Madrid: The Council of State recently held a meeting to study the situation on the various front lines. It is generally believed that the government will soon issue a general mobilization order to fight the Nationalist forces to a final victory. The government military headquarters issued a notice by radio at 9:20 PM tonight, stating, "According to the order issued by the Ministry of the Army, all trucks owned by residents in the capital area must be handed over by 10:00 PM tonight for military use. Those who disobey will be treated as rebels." The Ministry of the Army has also ordered all militiamen on leave to return to their units and await orders. In addition, the Ministry of the Army issued a war report at 9:45 PM, acknowledging that the rebel forces are pressing towards the south of Madrid but stating that the government troops are still resisting with all their might. In recent days, aircraft belonging to the Nationalist forces have continued to fly to the capital and its suburbs, and the sound of air raid sirens has been incessant. Nationalist aircraft have dropped many bombs, several of which have fallen into the army hospital in the town of Carabanchel, west of the capital. (Havas Telegram, 4th)

Non-Intervention Committee: Intense Debate Between Italian and Russian Representatives; Discussion of the Soviet Reply to Germany's Accusation; A Verbal Duel Nearly Breaks Up the Meeting 55

(London) At today's meeting of the Non-Intervention Committee for the Spanish Civil War, the main event was the discussion of the Soviet Union's reply to Germany's accusation of treaty violation. The representatives of Italy and the Soviet Union engaged in a verbal conflict in the meeting. After the Italian Ambassador to the UK spoke, the Soviet Ambassador to the UK, Maisky, immediately stated, "Italian Ambassador Grandi even mocks the tragic bombing of women and children in Madrid. I believe Mr. Grandi must be a great enemy of women and children, showing no sympathy for their suffering. I am not surprised by this, because the creed represented by Mr. Grandi is the most brutal and hateful war in the world. We have long seen examples of Italy completely disregarding human suffering. This is not the first time this has happened." The representatives of Italy and Germany at today's meeting unanimously refuted the Soviet Union's response, especially regarding the four Soviet Gorky-factory-produced bombers that arrived at the Getafe airfield in Madrid on September 18. Soviet Ambassador Maisky stated that there is no bomber or aircraft manufacturing plant named Gorky in the Soviet Union. Before the adjournment, the committee asked the Soviet Ambassador to further inquire with his home government about the points raised by Germany, and then submit the results to the committee. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

(London) After yesterday's meeting of the Non-Intervention Committee for the Spanish Civil War to discuss the Soviet Union's reply to Germany's accusation of treaty violation, a ten-page bulletin containing three appendices was released this morning, describing the intense debate that took place at yesterday's meeting. It is reported that the sub-committee plans to hold a meeting on the 9th of this month, and the general committee is scheduled to meet on November 12. The meeting originally scheduled for tomorrow afternoon has been canceled. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

France Plans to Actively Strengthen Border Defenses; The Maginot Line Extended to the Coast; Fortresses Built on the Franco-Swiss Border 56

(Paris) Today, French Deputy Prime Minister and Minister of National Defense Daladier declared that France's famous "Maginot Line" will be extended northward to the sea, and the solid fortifications built will be the same as those in Alsace-Lorraine. The area opposite the salient of the Ruhr region, which has not yet been armed due to the Treaty of 1814, will also have fortresses built. At the same time, the Jura region opposite the Swiss border will also be prepared with armaments to prevent invaders from violating Swiss neutrality. Daladier also stated that he intends to request an appropriation of 5 million pounds from the National Assembly to complete the border defenses. This project, with the extended portion, will be about 600 kilometers in length. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

(Paris) Daladier also announced that the government intends to adopt a youth compulsory military training system. All men over the age of seven or eight who have not enlisted should be forced to join training camps for short-term training. Youths under the age of eighteen should be required to take gymnastics as a compulsory subject in schools. The government will soon formulate laws for this military training system and submit them to the National Assembly for approval. The implementation of the law on nationalizing the arms industry, which was passed in July, has been quite satisfactory. In the past, military industries were concentrated in one place, which was inconvenient in the event of war. In the future, according to the law, 600 military supplies manufacturing plants can be set up throughout the country. (Havas Telegram, 4th)

Cabinet Reshuffle in Spain; Anarchists Appointed to the Cabinet; Anarchist Middle-of-the-Road Faction Joins the Collaboration 57

Madrid: The Caballero cabinet was reshuffled yesterday. The cabinet members include six Socialists, two Communists, one Left Republican, one Republican Unionist, one Basque Nationalist, and one Catalan Leftist, totaling twelve. Except for the Minister of Justice, Trianaes (Left Republican), and the Minister of Industry, Telegrafía (Socialist) (transferred to cabinet members without portfolio), all others remained in their original posts without any changes. However, four anarchists were newly added: Oliver is appointed Minister of Justice, Peiró is appointed Minister of Industry, Robert is appointed Minister of Commerce, and Mrs. Montseny is appointed Minister of Health (the Ministry of Commerce and the Ministry of Health are newly established). In addition, a Minister of Propaganda is added to position the Left Republican Esplá. After the cabinet reshuffle was completed, Prime Minister Caballero gave a speech, stating, "I believe that all forces that are anti-fascist should share government responsibility in the current environment. That is why I invited the anarchists to join the cabinet." He then issued a proclamation, stating, "Countrymen, all forces that are opposed to fascism have been recruited. I will tell the people the truth about the situation so that the people will rise up and defend the capital. What is the truth? It is that the enemy is now gathered around the capital. If the entire city of Madrid and the entire country of Spain are determined to resist the enemy, it will not be difficult to annihilate them, even if they are actively attacking." (Havas Telegram, 5th)

The Political Situation in France; Temporary Session of the National Assembly; Various Parties Determine Their Positions 58

(Paris) The second temporary session of the National Assembly is scheduled to open this afternoon. Parliamentary groups of various parties held meetings this morning to determine their positions on the government's proposals, especially the reform of the financial system for provinces and cities. When the parliamentary group of the orthodox Socialist Party opened the meeting, it first listed all the issues that the National Assembly should discuss during this session and explained that the government authorities' tax reform plan should be submitted first so that the Senate could submit it for discussion during the National Assembly's debate on the budget bill in order to save time. Finance Minister Olivol also stated that the government has decided to make every effort to compromise in accordance with the rules of procedure to ensure that the next budget bill can be passed this year. When the parliamentary group of the Communist Party held a meeting, it expressed support for the speech given by the party secretary-general, Thorez, on the 30th of last month, advocating the cessation of the sealing off of the Spanish government. Regarding this matter, the party's congressman, Bellay, has submitted a question to the Secretariat of the National Assembly and requested the National Assembly to submit it for discussion within a short period of time. In addition, the party also intends to raise a number of other questions, advocating effective means to dissolve various fascist groups and advocating that those who "sabotage" social laws must be punished. The party's parliamentary group also issued a communiqué after the meeting, stating, "The party's parliamentary group will actively defend the above-mentioned proposals and will urge the government to unswervingly implement the political program set by the Popular Front, so that this political program can be fully implemented." (Havas Telegram, 5th)

The Political Situation in Japan is Unstable; The Military Advocates Abolishing Party Politics; The Seiyukai Rejects Fascism 59

(Tokyo) The Japanese army has recently expressed its opinion advocating the abolition of party politics. The reactions of the Seiyukai and Minseitō parties to this advocacy are now becoming stronger. Activities to consolidate a common front to protect the constitutional system are now quite strong. Cabinet party members have also declared their determination to defend party politics. This wave of unrest in the political world is now rapidly expanding. However, according to general observation, since the above-mentioned problem is quite serious, if the opinion of eliminating party politics continues to spread, it will make the determination to protect party politics even higher, and this may cause a crisis. Therefore, before the recess of the next national food season next spring, the opposing side does not seem to be making further opposition to party politics. (Central News Agency, 5th)

(Nanjing) After the issue of reforming the parliamentary system arose, the Seiyukai was greatly impacted. As a result, the voice of advocating the protection of constitutional government within the party suddenly became stronger. At the meeting of the Policy Research Committee on the 4th, all members expressed strong opinions, opposing fascism. Unanimously, it was agreed that the attitude of political parties has always been too passive, so there are often voices criticizing political parties. At this time, political parties must clearly express their own views and decisively reject European and American fascism. The Policy Research Committee should base its spirit on this and quickly decide on concrete methods. As a result of the discussion, it was decided that Chairman Sunada would draft countermeasures for the Seiyukai in times of emergency, and after obtaining the party's approval, declare it to the inside and outside. (Domei News Agency, 3rd)

Japan-Siam Treaty Abolished 60

(Tokyo) The Siamese Minister to Japan, Nakusha, visited Vice Minister Horinouchi at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the morning of the 5th and handed over a note addressed to Foreign Minister Arita, which stated, "The Siamese government has decided to abolish the Japan-Siam Treaty of Commerce and Navigation and the attached protocol signed in Bangkok on February 10, 1924. I am hereby instructed by my government to notify the Japanese government that, in accordance with Article 20 of the treaty, the current treaty will remain in effect for one year after the notification of the abolition of the treaty. This should be understood." The Minister also added that the abolition applies not only to Japan, but to all countries that have signed similar treaties with Siam. Vice Minister Horinouchi replied that the Japanese government's intention would be answered later, but in order to avoid a no-treaty situation, a new treaty would be concluded during the effective period, which would be beneficial to both parties. (Domei News Agency, 5th)

Communist Leader Beheaded in Hamburg, Germany 61

(Berlin) Communist leader Andreas in Hamburg, Germany, was beheaded today. Andreas was sentenced to death in July of this year in connection with a case of insulting the Nazi Party several years ago. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

New Parliament Building Completed in Japan; Construction Lasted Seventeen Years and Cost 25 Million 62

(Tokyo) The new parliament building, which took 17 years and cost 25 million to complete, was officially opened by the Japanese Emperor on the 5th. The Emperor wore an army dress uniform and left the Imperial Palace at 10:00 AM, arriving at the new parliament building at 10:05 AM. In the audience hall on the second floor, he listened to the Minister of Finance Baba, the President of the House of Peers Konoe, and the Speaker of the House of Representatives Tomita present the progress of the completion, etc. After a short break, he visited the various rooms of the parliament building under the leadership of President Konoe and decided to hold a celebration from the 6th to the 11th. However, a purification ceremony was held at 11:00 AM on the morning of the 4th. The participants were officials from the Ministry of Finance's Construction Bureau, the Vice Presidents of the House of Peers and the House of Representatives, and more than 80 other construction-related personnel. The ceremony was solemn. (Domei News Agency, 5th)

Chiang and Yan Meet in Luoyang to Discuss Joint Communist Suppression and Congratulate Chiang on His Birthday; Yan Returns to Taiyuan and Reports Opinions on National Affairs 64

Taiyuan Dispatch: Military Affairs Commission Vice Chairman Yan Xishan, accompanied by Xu Yongchang, Director of the Qingxiang Office of Shanxi Province, Chuan Zuoyi, Chairman of the Suiyuan Provincial Government, and attendants including Xue Chongxi, Chief of the Social Affairs Section, and Liang Jiaohou, Secretary, a party of twelve, flew from Taiyuan to Xi'an via a Boeing aircraft on the 30th of last month. After arriving that day, they took a special Longhai Railway military train eastward at 8 PM, arriving in Luoyang at 7:40 AM on the 31st. After disembarking, they immediately met with Chairman Chiang at the Luoyang Military Branch School. At 9 AM, they celebrated Chairman Chiang's birthday. Before 11 AM, Chiang visited Yan for talks. At 7:30 PM, Chiang hosted a special banquet at Siwei Hall. After discussing joint Communist suppression arrangements for Shanxi, Suiyuan, Shaanxi, and Ningxia, and celebrating Chiang's birthday in Luoyang, Yan, accompanied by Xu, Chuan, and all attendants, took off by plane at 12 AM on the 1st, arriving in Taiyuan at 1:40 PM. They circled twice over the city before landing at the airfield outside the North Gate. After learning of Yan's confirmed return to Taiyuan, military and government officials from Zhao Daiwen, Chairman of the Provincial Government, and Yang Aiyuan, Commander-in-Chief, down to Yan's wife and son, all went to the airfield to welcome him. After Yan disembarked, the welcoming personnel stepped forward to greet him, and Yan returned the greetings. After a brief exchange, he took a car back to the government office. Xu and Chuan also returned to their private residences on Dongbian Street and Toutao Lane, North Gate Street.

According to a member of Yan's entourage, the details of arriving in Luoyang were as follows: "When Vice Chairman Yan flew from Taiyuan to Xi'an on the 30th, those who welcomed him at the airfield included Vice Commander Zhang, Director Yang, and other senior military officers. After disembarking, they went to Zhuiwei for a rest at Director Yang's invitation. At 6 PM, they attended a banquet hosted by Zhang, Yang, and Shao. At 8 PM, they took a special train eastward with Vice Commander Zhang, He Yaozu, Xu Yongchang, Fu Zuoyi, Gao Guizi, and Gao Shuangcheng, arriving in Luoyang at 7:40 AM on the 31st. After disembarking, they immediately met with Chairman Chiang at the Luoyang Military Branch School. Chairman Chiang wore military fatigues and was in excellent spirits. At 11 AM, various circles in Luoyang hosted a banquet for Chairman Chiang and his wife at Siwei Hall in the Military School, with about a hundred participants. The Military School specially prepared a Vice Chairman's office for Yan. Before 11 AM, Chiang visited Yan in casual clothes for talks. At 7:30 PM, Chiang hosted a banquet at Siwei Hall. When Chairman Chiang and Vice Commander Zhang saw him off at the airfield when they took off from Luoyang today (the 1st), Chiang and Yan talked and walked at the airfield for about ten minutes before boarding the plane and taking off." After Yan returned to Taiyuan, he attended the memorial week meeting of the Shanxi and Suiyuan provincial governments this morning (the 2nd) and reported his impressions after meeting Chiang in Luoyang and his opinions on national affairs, as follows: "This trip to Xi'an and Luoyang was very rewarding. I feel that everything in the country is making great progress. In particular, the population of Xi'an is increasing rapidly, the streets are neat, and land prices are soaring, which is very significant. Grain prices in both places have risen due to the planting of winter wheat to seventy percent, but after government regulation, they have also fallen. As for the future of the country, the central government still adheres to the principle of seeking national salvation through limited compromise and striving for reconciliation. No matter what kind of violent invasion comes, it will resolutely resist to defend the national territory." (November 2nd)

Tension Rises Again on the Chahar-Suiyuan Border; Bandit Troops Advance Westward; Li Shouxin and Wang Ying's Troops Serve as the Backbone of the Invasion of Suiyuan; Rehe Bandit Troops Move to Support Li and Wang; Residents of Shangyi's Nanchaoqian Have Fled En Masse 65

Shangdu Dispatch: Recently, the situation on the Chahar-Suiyuan border has been tense and relaxed at times, and people are worried and uncertain. Recently, Wang Ying's bandit troops have been trained by a certain party and are responsible for the main role in invading Suiyuan. In addition, Li Shouxin, the most trusted puppet army commander of Zhangbei of a certain party, is also an important figure in the westward invasion, and has also obtained the power of a certain party to supply the Chahar bandit troops with military supplies, coordinating with Wang Ying to advance together. Therefore, the Chahar-Suiyuan border has recently shown signs of tension again, and the bandit troops are advancing westward. According to people from Zhangbei, the total number of Rehe bandit troops assembled in the hunting grounds has exceeded 10,000. Recently, they have received orders from a certain party to transfer 6,000 people from the assembled bandit troops to Duolun by the 10th of this month. The Rehe bandit troops currently stationed in Duolun, numbering about 4,000, have also moved westward, with the destination being the Baochang-Kangbao area, approaching Shangdu to support Wang Ying and Li Shouxin's invasion of Suiyuan. Now, bandit troops are constantly transporting materials between Duolun, Baochang, and Kangbao.

The residents living in the Shangdu-Shangyi (ie Daqinggou)-Nanchaoqian area are disturbed by the frequent mobilization of bandit troops and busy transportation. Moreover, when bandits pass through the area, they either demand food and fodder or requisition strong men and mules and horses. If the supply is delayed even slightly, they are whipped immediately and arbitrarily harassed. Farmers' sheep and chickens are slaughtered and eaten at will. Generally, those with some assets cannot bear the disturbance, so they have mostly fled, mostly to Zhangjiakou or Datong. Only the poor people are unable to move and take refuge, and can only obey fate and let them trample on them. Li Shouxin, the puppet army commander of the main force of the westward invasion, in order to understand the true situation of the troops' strength and military supplies, specifically set out from Zhangbei on the 6th of this month, and planned to first go to Sanbaogou-Daqinggou-Nanchaoqian area to inspect the deployment of his troops in the western Chahar area, whether the defense works of the positions were solid, and to give speeches to the soldiers at the front to encourage the Zhang bandits. Secondly, he went to Gonghui-Mantouying to inspect his support troops, and then returned to Zhangbei. Whether the number of troops was sufficient, whether the clothing was neat, and whether the food, fodder, and ammunition were sufficient would be actively sought and supplemented after this inspection in order to increase its strength.

The military supplies needed by the puppet bandits in northern Chahar are concentrated in Zhangbei as a distribution point, and the number of goods transported in and out every day is endless and cannot be counted. According to statistics, on the 31st of last month alone, Li Shouxin used 45 trucks to transport a large amount of military supplies from Zhangbei, 13 trucks to Daqinggou, including 1 truck of rifles, a total of 18 boxes, 10 rifles per box, a total of 180 rifles, 3 trucks of artillery shells and bullets, 1 truck of tents, 3 trucks of gasoline and kerosene, and 5 trucks of coal; 16 trucks to Nanchaoqian, including 4 trucks of bullets and artillery shells, 6 trucks of gasoline and kerosene, and 6 trucks of coal. In addition, there were 7 trucks of coal and 4 trucks of bullets to Shangdu, and a total of 6 trucks of firearms and bullets to Jiabusi. (2nd)

He Jian Returns to Hunan from Nanjing Yesterday; He Has Resigned from His Post as Pacification Commissioner 66

Nanjing Dispatch: He Jian flew from Hunan to Wuhan and then to Nanjing on the 28th of last month to present three aircraft to the central government and congratulate Chairman Chiang on his birthday. Now that the official business is completed, he took a plane back to Hunan at 8 AM on the 5th. It is said that He is very busy presiding over Hunan's provincial affairs, and the government has recently established many new border area pacification agencies. The Changsha Pacification Headquarters seems to have no need to be retained, so he submitted a document to the Military Affairs Commission two months ago, requesting the abolition of the Changsha Pacification Headquarters. Now that the abolition of the headquarters has been realized, he believes that he has returned to his original position.

Yuehan Railway: Two Train Collisions in the Chen County Section; More Than Thirty People Killed in the Dengjiawan Tragedy; More Than Ten People Killed or Injured in the Donglou Bridge Accident 67

Guangzhou Dispatch: In the past three months, unfortunate incidents have occurred frequently on the country's railways. Since the Yuehan Railway started direct trains, there have been four train collisions. The accident on the 22nd of last month involving the 94th passenger-freight mixed train in the Leheng area near Taipingli and Dengjiawan was particularly tragic. The Yue Railway Office in Guangzhou sent Cheng Xiaogang, Director of the Transportation Department, to the scene of the accident to investigate. After Cheng arrived at Dengjiatang, he inspected and registered the bodies of the victims separately and prepared 36 coffins for burial. In addition, there were 6 unknown passengers who were buried locally in Dengjiatang. The soldiers of the special platoon of the 199th Regiment of the 67th Division who were killed and injured were taken back to the division headquarters for coffin burial. The vehicles that collided on that day were completely disintegrated, and the adjacent carriages were also damaged. The locomotives were transported to the Chenzhou Locomotive Factory for repair. Ling Hongdong, Director of the Yuehan Railway Bureau, also went to Chenzhou at the end of last month and then went to Dengjiatang to inspect everything. After several days of investigation, he left Chenzhou and returned to Wuhan on the 31st of last month. The Ministry of Railways sent Jin Shiyi, Director of the Business Department, and Niu Xiaoxian, Director of the Finance Department, to the south to investigate the situation along the way. Jin and Niu arrived in Guangzhou on the 1st and inspected the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway on the 2nd. Unexpectedly, the Dengjiatang case had not yet been investigated, and on the 1st of this month, there was another train collision at the Donglou Bridge Station near Chenzhou. The Yuehan Railway Office in Guangzhou immediately sent a hand-cranked engineering vehicle to rescue and repair the tracks. It was found that the location of the collision was near the Xiaoshuipu Donglou Bridge Station, which is more than ten kilometers north of Bang County. First, a military train carrying soldiers opened northward from Lechang. When it arrived near Donglou Bridge, there was a slope with low drops on both ends. Vehicles encountering or approaching on both sides were often not easy to see from a distance. When the military train drove to the bottom of the slope, at about 7 AM one morning, a northbound passenger-freight train from Yuehan came from behind (the train departed from Guangzhou at 11 PM on the 30th). Because the locomotive was a new-style express train, the speed was higher than that of the old locomotive. When it drove to Donglou Bridge Station, it was blocked by the height of the slope and did not find the military train in front. Finally, it caught up at the mileage of 602 to 650 of Donglou Bridge Station and pushed against the rear of the military train, destroying the military train in front. At the same time, the northbound locomotive and two freight cars also derailed and pressed against the orange railing, fortunately not falling into the river. After the two trains collided, more than ten people died on the spot. After the accident, Donglou Bridge Station was blocked by the stranded vehicles, and traffic was interrupted for a time. The direct train from Wuchang to the south could not pass when it drove to the station, so it had to stop abruptly, and then took the passengers from Guangzhou back to Wuhan. At the same time, the northbound accident locomotive was also repaired and took the southbound train passengers to Guangzhou. Therefore, the passengers on this southbound train did not arrive safely at Huangsha Station in Guangzhou until 12 noon on the 2nd. After the damaged tracks and sleepers were repaired by the engineering vehicle, the section of the road could be operated as usual on the 3rd. After reporting to the Ministry of Railways, it immediately telegraphed the two directors Jin and Niu, who were in Guangdong, to investigate the train collision at Donglou Station when they went north, so as to find ways to remedy the safety of future train operations. (November 3rd)

Songjiang: Robbery of Cooperative 68

At the Yangdianxiang Purchasing Cooperative in Dongshi, Yexie Town, Punan, five or six bandits suddenly came the night before last, speaking a mixture of local and Hakka dialects, each holding guns and breaking into the house. One bandit pointed a gun at the accountant, Ding, to monitor him and prevent him from making a sound. The remaining bandits dispersed to search for loot. Manager Jiang Heming was lying in the next room. Hearing the sound, he immediately escaped through the back door, but was hit in the waist and back by a wooden stick by the bandit on lookout, and fell to the ground. At this time, the neighbors also heard the sound, so they rang the alarm. Knowing that the matter was not good, the bandits did not have time to carry the loot and roared away.

Wuxi: Loading and Unloading Problem Solved 70

The No. 3 Spinning Mill of Shenxin in this county recently rented vacant land next to the Xiyangqi of Wuxi Station from the Jinghu Railway to build a new Ren warehouse and hired workers to load and unload goods. The railway porters rose up to dispute, causing a dispute. Now, after repeated mediation by the Railway Bureau, it has been resolved. Both parties have signed a work contract. The mediation principle is that goods such as cotton yarn, cloth, rice, wheat, beans, and grain are carried from the freight car to the platform or loaded from the platform into the freight car by railway workers, calculated at 9 cents per ton, for a period of one year.

Danyang: Robbery Near Erling 71

Tang Xiaosheng, an administrator of the Qingxiang Office in the third district of the county, was collecting factory funds from opium smokers on the afternoon of the 1st of this month when Tang Zhanxiu, Tang Jinfu, Tang Shengfu, Tang Fajin, etc., learned of it, knocked Tang Xiaosheng down and tied him up, filled his mouth with mud, and searched for and robbed him of more than 20 yuan of fund banknotes and foreign money. Later, passers-by Tang Boying and Cai Suolong saw it, untied him, removed the mud from his mouth, and asked about the robbery. Tang Xiaosheng immediately reported it to the Erling Public Security Sub-station, which sent a shock to arrest the principal offenders Tang Jinfu and Tang Zhanxiu. The remaining ones escaped. It is heard that the sub-station has transferred the two offenders to the General Bureau for transfer to the county for handling according to law.

Bandit Alert in Shaojiacun 72

Shao Wang, a woman from Shaojiacun, Baoying Township, District 1, outside the West Gate, is engaged in farming and has a well-to-do family, which has been coveted by bandits. At about 9 PM the night before last, two thieves armed with axes went to Shao's house to rob. Wang was held by the bandits and was slashed in the face with an axe. Her daughter-in-law, Tang, was also affected. The bandits then robbed and roared away. Afterwards, Shao reported the case to the county and asked to arrest the bandits and recover the stolen goods.

Gaoyou: Stabilize the Exchange Rate of Legal Tender 74

Before the Mid-Autumn Festival, the exchange rate of legal tender to copper coins in this county was 3,250 copper coins per yuan. Unexpectedly, it has gradually fallen recently to 2,950 copper coins, and there is still a tendency to continue falling, which has a great impact. In view of this, the county government specifically announced on the 2nd that it would still follow the Ministry's regulations of exchanging 3,000 copper coins per yuan, and must not fall below the statutory decree of the Ministry, and ordered the County Chamber of Commerce to instruct the industry associations to comply.

Shouxin District's Aircraft Purchase Donation 75

The county government believes that the district offices and agencies have not complied with the order to pay the donation for purchasing aircraft for birthday celebrations, and recently sent police to the districts to collect the money in order to remit it and avoid delay.

Liuhe: Tragedy of Burning a Fetus to Death 76

Recently, the county has been dry due to the weather, and fires have occurred for days. Unexpectedly, a fire broke out outside the South City again at 4 PM yesterday. After hearing the news, the fire brigades rushed to rescue. At that time, the Nancha Township People's School was training. Suddenly, they saw black smoke billowing in front. Wang Bowu, the principal of the school, and Song Peisen, the instructor, bravely led the trainees to rescue. At that time, because the southeast wind was strong, the fire was even more intense. In a short while, eight families, including Jin Guanglong, Hu Sanzhang, Zhang Jiating, Wang Haozi, Qiang Jiasheng, and Wang Youdian, were burned to the ground. It is estimated that more than 20 houses were burned down, with losses of thousands of yuan. Among them, Wang Haozi's eight-month-old fetus was not taken out in time, resulting in being buried in the fire. The situation was extremely tragic.

Hangzhou: Drawing River Water to Relieve Drinking Water 77

Since entering autumn, Hangzhou has been dry for a long time, and it has been almost two months. Although there has been a welcome rain recently, the water volume is still not very sufficient. In order to prevent drought disasters, the Construction Department plans to open the 300-horsepower water pump installed at the Zhakou Pumping Station for ten days to pump the water from the Qiantang River into the river to facilitate irrigation and fill the urban area with firewood. The machine can pump 1.5 million gallons of water per hour, 30 million gallons of water per day, and the cost is 1,500 yuan, which is borne equally by the provincial and municipal governments. It is scheduled to start pumping water on the 6th. However, according to the chemical inspection report of the Waterworks, the salinity of the Qiantang River water has reached 8 parts per thousand, and it is not suitable for drinking or irrigation. Therefore, it is planned to pump it in when the salinity is reduced to 4 parts per thousand for application.

Shaoxing: The County Government Plans to Build the Keyan Road 78

The county government's plan to build the Keyan Highway specially convened a joint meeting of the Finance Committee and the Design Committee yesterday, and decided to pass it according to the original plan and entrust it to the Xiaoshao Automobile Company for construction.

Ningbo: A Large Amount of Money Was Stolen from Dayuan Bank 79

The Dayuan Bank on Jiangxia Street in this port has always been operating steadily. There are currently 13 partners, 7 apprentices, and 3 clerks. Next to it is the empty house of the bankrupt Yuankang Bank. The night before last, the bank happened to have a large sum of money placed in a silver box. After the partner Fan, who was in charge of the silver box, locked it, he went to bed separately. Unexpectedly, when he got up the next morning, he saw a large hole chiseled in the wall of the adjacent empty house. Knowing that something was wrong, he rushed to see the silver box and saw that it had been opened. He checked the national currency and found that more than 5,000 yuan was lost. He reported the information to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau and the Ningbo Detective Team, and each sent detectives to the scene to investigate. Because the incident was bizarre, they are conducting a detailed and strict investigation.

Major Fire in Guoju Town, Zhenhai 80

In the seventh Bao area of Guoju Town, Zhenhai, there is a large Xu family house with more than 30 buildings and bungalows. On the morning of the 2nd, it was not careful about fire, and the entire house was reduced to ashes. The loss was no less than 10,000 yuan. Except for the three rooms of the Jing family that were burned, the other neighbors were fortunately not affected.

Special Letter from Peiping

The Ancient City of Beiping Under the Sound of Wheels – Random Notes on a Parade of Japanese Troops Through the City 81

For the last eight or nine days, the large-scale military exercises of the Japanese troops has thrust the area around Beiping-Tianjin-Fengtai into a state of unease and alarm. The suburbs of Beiping have long been disturbed and restless, with everyone on edge. However, the city of Beiping itself has been able to maintain a semblance of normality due to being under the supervision of the various foreign legations. Although the sound of artillery fire has been faintly audible throughout the day, peace and prosperity, with singing and dancing, has continued as before. However, the Japanese troops have not abandoned their intention to demonstrate their power to the residents of the city. Therefore, on the day before the conclusion of their "autumn maneuvers" (the 3rd), they held a parade through the city.

The route of the parade was from the Chaoyangmen, on the northeast corner of the city, through the prosperous areas of Dongsi, Dongdan, East and West Chang'an Streets, Xidan, and so on. At Xidan, the procession divided into two streams. One went south to Xuanwumen, through Zhangyimen Avenue, to Guang'anmen on the southwest corner of the city; the other went north to Xizhimen on the northwest corner of the city. The length of the route was about ten to twenty li in total. The parade was carried out in a way that completely simulated the retreat and pursuit of combat, with the front teams retreating and the rear teams in hot pursuit. In this retreat and pursuit, the intention of the parade through the city was implied.

At about 8 o'clock, the team simulating a defeated retreat began to enter Chaoyangmen. At the front were three small motorcycle trikes, each carrying two people, one driving and one holding a machine gun. Behind them were three sedan cars. Each car was occupied by three to five officers. A glimpse revealed that most had a short mustache on their lips. After this, large trucks full of Japanese troops came in a whirlwind, one after another. After a slight break after the trucks, another small motorcycle appeared. After this, tanks, large trucks, supply vehicles, small motorcycles, sedan cars, artillery vehicles, and so on came on continuously, sometimes in teams of several vehicles, sometimes with slight gaps, the rumble of their engines deafening. The dust raised by the vehicles shook the roads, and the houses trembled. This continued for about three hours, until it ended at half past eleven. Statistics show that there were more than a hundred vehicles of all kinds, and about 1,500 to 1,600 officers and soldiers. The exteriors of all these vehicles were uniformly painted in grayish-yellow. The large trucks full of soldiers were entirely draped in camouflage grass, closely resembling the situation in combat against aerial bombardment. The tops of the tanks were mostly equipped with anti-aircraft machine guns, with one person sitting beside them, preparing to aim and shoot at the sky. The uniforms of the officers and soldiers were all grayish-yellow, the same color as the vehicles. Many wore masks and glasses, and the red bands on the officers' hats were extraordinarily bright, most striking in the rolling dust and sand. It was also heard that hundreds of infantrymen entered the city through Guangqumen.

Everywhere the Japanese troops passed, the sides of the streets were crowded with spectators, but the pushing and urging of the police was of no avail. This reporter witnessed three people, the owner and his servants, from a sesame cake shop argue and quarrel because they had all gone to the roadside to watch, resulting in the loss of some cakes. He also saw a silk shop closing its doors at that time, with the entire staff watching from the doorway. Pedestrians on the road, except those who had pressing matters to attend to, also mostly stopped to watch, and their expressions were mostly worried. For even the most composed individuals found it difficult to calm their minds and go about their business in the midst of this rumbling of vehicles.

At this time, the expatriates from "friendly nations" were mostly in high spirits. North of Dongdan, there were rows of "friendly nation" elementary school students, dressed very neatly, as if attending a grand ceremony. As the Japanese troops passed by, they cheered and applauded loudly. The sun-shaped national flags of their countries were also hung high at the entrances of various private residences. Particularly striking among these were three locations: the Zhonghe Pharmacy on Dongdan Avenue, the Dongya Bookstore on the same street, and a certain shop near Wangfu and the adjacent Wangfujing Street. The flags hung in these three places were extraordinarily large and new, seemingly recently made. "Friendly nation" women, dressed neatly and made up with rouge and powder, and their backs slightly hunched, dragged their thick, wide clogs, walking back and forth on the street like shuttles. Their hearts seemed to have boundless joy, with no way to vent it, causing my fellow Chinese compatriots watching on the sides of the road to avert their eyes and comment.

Among the columns of Japanese military vehicles, there were often American cars mixed in. Sometimes they were sedan cars, with one or two American people sitting inside, and sometimes they were also American women. According to this reporter's estimation, there were a total of three women driving themselves. Most of these American people were probably news reporters, followed by members of the diplomatic corps. Ordinary expatriates who followed along purely out of curiosity were probably not many. Or they were freight trucks, with three to five soldiers sitting on them, leaning back with their legs crossed, sometimes smiling. There were about ten to twenty of these freight trucks mixed in with the Japanese military vehicles. When the Chinese people saw them, their worry was slightly tempered by excitement. They often responded with a bitter smile. This kind of mentality is also the norm. It is heard that they were also conducting exercises outside the city, and were returning on this day. When this reporter walked past the East Legation Quarter, he saw that expatriates from other countries were also coming out one after another to watch in various places. It can be seen from this that they were concerned about this parade by the Japanese troops.

Sports News

Two World Professional Tennis Giants, Tilden and Vines, Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday; Performance at 1 PM Today; Will Take Original Ship to Hong Kong Tonight; Return to the US by Original Ship After Manila Performance 82

Two giants of the world professional tennis scene, Tilden and Vines, who once held the reins of world amateur tennis, and Ms. Harbutt, a professional female tennis player, arrived here yesterday at 8:00 AM aboard the President Lincoln from Japan. Yesterday, they were busy with social engagements and sightseeing. Starting at 1:00 PM today, at the Canavero court at 153 Route Notre Dame, the two gentlemen will give a ticketed public performance. Tonight, they will take the original ship to Hong Kong and then on to Manila. A brief account of the situation is as follows:

Arrived in Shanghai Early

The Lincoln, originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai this morning, arrived a day early, entering port yesterday morning. Among those welcoming them at the new Customs Wharf were Canavero, a local professional tennis player, and Boer from Puda Trading Company, which is in charge of this business venture. After exiting the new Customs Wharf, Tilden and Vines went directly to the International Hotel to rest, arriving around 9:30 AM. Both are tall and robust, showing no signs of travel fatigue.

Yesterday's Social Engagements

At noon yesterday, the two gentlemen attended a banquet hosted by the American Club on Fuzhou Road. Last night, Citibank also hosted a welcome banquet. At 9:00 PM, they attended the opening ceremony of the new "Shall We Dance" dance hall on Jing'an Temple Road, keeping them very busy. From 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM in the afternoon, they practiced at the Notre Dame Road court to stretch their muscles. Canavero and local star players, including McGer Tagping and Xian Daimingfa, also participated.

Today's Performance

Starting at 1:00 PM this afternoon, the two gentlemen will perform singles and doubles matches at the Brocklin court at 153 Route Notre Dame. Ms. Harbutt will not be able to perform due to the lack of an opponent. The order of the performance is as follows:

Singles: Tilden vs. Vines - Three Sets

Doubles: Dai Mingfa & Wang Miaosong vs. Cai Houfa & Wang Miaoxing - Two Sets

Doubles: Tilden & Tao Maonan vs. Vines & Canavero - Three Sets

Vines' Remarks

Vines made the following remarks during the trip: Tilden and I performed four times together in Tokyo, with each performance attracting around 10,000 spectators. After leaving Tokyo, we toured Nagoya, Osaka, and other places, continuing to perform. We held so-called "instructional" performances in Japan, using only one referee. Japan's top player, Yamagishi, participated in the "instructional" performances multiple times. According to my observation, Yamagishi's skills rank between eighth and fifteenth in the world. The techniques of Japanese tennis players are becoming increasingly modernized. Their only shortcomings are a lack of imagination and speed. As for the future of professional tennis, I am very optimistic. However, the confrontation between the amateur and professional worlds may not occur for at least five or six years because the organization of professional tennis associations is not yet sound.

Among the world's amateur players, Pancho Segura still slightly outranks Budge Patty and Gardnar Mulloy. However, Patty and Mulloy are improving rapidly and will one day surpass Segura. Whether England can retain the Davis Cup next year depends on whether Segura maintains his amateur status. The chances for the United States, Australia, and Germany are equal. France's strength is still insufficient. Coen is more advanced than before, but Vines has not met Coen in two years. The travel plan has been set. There will be a singles performance in Hong Kong, followed by Manila. As for the trip to South Africa, it is unlikely to happen because there has been no contact between the two parties. Therefore, after the Manila performance, we will return to the United States. Tilden has scheduled matches in the US, and Vines is eager to return home to see his wife and daughters.

Tilden's Remarks

According to Mr. Tilden, this is the first time that Vines and I have visited the Far East for sightseeing. Everything feels vibrant. We stayed in Japan for about a month, performing more than ten times in Tokyo, Osaka, Nagoya, and other places, and received much praise from the local people. Chinese tennis has also made considerable progress in recent years. I have been involved in tennis for thirty-five years, starting at the age of seven when I was studying at primary school and have enjoyed it ever since. When asked about the trip to Australia and whether it had been canceled, and whether he could perform again when passing through Shanghai on the return trip, Tilden said that the trip to Australia had been canceled. The southward journey will end in Manila, and we will take the original ship back home. We must return to the United States by Christmas. Therefore, whether we can stop in Shanghai on the way back will have to be telegraphed from Manila. He hopes to perform in Shanghai again, and perhaps it will be possible.

Brief Biographies of Tilden and Vines

Tilden is 43 years old this year and began his tennis career at the age of 17 in 1919. While studying at the University of Pennsylvania, he had already become one of the famous figures in the world of tennis. He dominated the tennis world for 17 years and is still one of the strongest players in the world. He graduated from university in 1922. In 1920, he won the US Open singles title, winning it six consecutive years until 1926 when he was defeated by Lacoste of France. He won it again in 1927. He won the Wimbledon title three times in 1920, 1921, and 1930. He was 38 years old the last time, while Tilden was 28 years old.

Vines is 23 years old this year. In 1931, at the age of 18, he won the US Open singles title. He won it again in 1932. In the same year, he also won the Wimbledon title. He got married at the age of 10. Experts observe that, even among the best in the world today, including Pancho Segura, few can defeat Vines. Vines is still young and has a bright future.

Social Affairs Bureau Issues Circular to Schools Requiring Students to Undergo Tuberculosis Screening; Among 428 Students Screened, 25% Suffer from Lung Disease 95

The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau issued a circular to all schools in the city, stating: "According to a report submitted by Gu Yuqi, Dean of the Private Datong Medical College, in view of the importance of public health and the urgent need to promote tuberculosis prevention, the college has decided to conduct tuberculosis X-ray screening. To promote widespread screening, each person is charged only one yuan for the procedure. Students in secondary schools are charged only 80 cents each time, and primary school students are charged 60 cents. From September 1st to the end of September, a total of 428 people came to the college for screening, including 216 students. Among them, eight students had recovered from lung disease, and seventeen were in the early stages, accounting for a strong 24%. This phenomenon is alarming, considering the small number of students screened. The college originally focused on screening students and teachers. However, since the number of students is limited, and no teachers have been screened, it is necessary to actively promote this work. It is proposed that the bureau again issue a circular to all schools in the city to implement screening in order to emphasize public health and prevent the spread of disease. A form is attached for your reference. Therefore, as the college had previously requested the former Municipal Education Bureau to issue a circular to all schools to implement X-ray screening of students' lungs, we are now issuing this circular and requiring all schools to strictly comply."
