Shen Bao Literary Supplement

The Most Beautiful Short Letter 201

— Original by German author Bruno Frank

The most touching letter I know of is the one that Ivan Turgenev wrote to Leo Tolstoy shortly before his death.

Here is the letter: -

"Bougival, June 27th or 28th, 1883.

Dear and kind Lev Nikolayevich! I have not written to you for a long time because I have been, and in fact still am, lying on my deathbed. As for regaining my health – that is completely hopeless, and it is not worth thinking about. I am actually writing to you simply to make you understand how proud I have been to be your contemporary and to make one last and sincere request of you. — My friend, return to literary work! Because your talent comes to you from the source of all other things, as you know. How happy I would be if I felt certain that my request would affect you!

I am a 'finished' man – many doctors do not even know what to call my illness – 'neuralgic gastralgia with gout'. I can neither walk, nor eat, nor sleep, so what is left for me to do? Even speaking about it is enough to suffer. My friend, great writer of the Russian land – heed my request. —"

How passionately hope surges from these few lines! The emotion of life, in such a state, emits such a farewell greeting, how precious are all the wishes! Renan (also a member of the literary group in Paris to which Turgenev belonged) once described the nineteenth century as a gentle and beautiful period, with a climate suitable for the development of art and science, which would inevitably be followed by a rough period. Ah, yes, the rough period followed as he said. The nineteenth century, the last to bid farewell to ancient culture, seems to be a paradise of harmony and wisdom to those who have been exiled and experienced great suffering as they look back on it.

Literary critics with strict standards do not acknowledge that Turgenev's grave deserves a place in the holy ground of their great deceased writers. They do not consider him a genius, but merely a talented person. This is indeed the case. He was despised by the profound genius of Russia, Dostoevsky. It is true that Dostoevsky unexpectedly visited him, cursing him in front of the startled man for committing a dishonorable act, and declaring that placing him in a lower position than someone like Turgenev was the most severe curse that heaven could inflict upon him. Turgenev, however, was well-suited to be with the group of famous writers he met in Paris—such as Flaubert, the Goncourt brothers, Zola, Taine, and Renan—all of whom had the same soul and resembled him, and all of whom loved him. They called him the gentle giant (Le doux géant). The keynote of his character was humanity, built upon a foundation of human emotion and a discerning knowledge of the doubtfulness of facts. Observing oneself is also fitting. Without indulging in false and absurd dreams, but instead persisting without retreating in life, being benevolent without fear – this is a difficult ideal to grasp as an encouragement, especially for an era like the one we live in, an era whose typical figures are utterly despicable – these people are foolish, corrupt, and at the same time intoxicated with gaudy rhetoric.

With less extravagance and artificiality than Turgenev's letter, they would amount to nothing. "I have been and still am lying on my deathbed," in his opinion, was already a bit too much, too forceful, so he added the touching "in fact," a kind of annoying little phrase, also a kind of apologetic expression that he had to tell himself in such a serious and touching state. His symptoms must have been terrible, with the entire nerve surface of the skin swollen, constantly experiencing agonizing pain. But there is not a single word about the pain! He begins by openly describing his situation and slightly satirizing the doctors, but immediately dismisses it: "Even speaking about it is enough to suffer."

What he means is: Tolstoy might feel uncomfortable. In his knowledge, familiar with the human alienation due to doubt, which separates individuals, he avoids evoking an emotional response from another person for more than a minute. But he also knows that everyone will be uncomfortable if their sympathy and pity are exploited. Because in this sentence, he does not directly appeal to Tolstoy, he omits the pronoun and speaks generally. This omitted pronoun, in its perfection and solemnity, can surpass all publicly written works and spoken words of the current year in Europe.

Now, let's return to the vow written by the hand of this person destined to die: "How proud I have been to be your contemporary." How admirable the humility, how deep the heartfelt reverence, to have such a turn of phrase! Does it not mean, and even more than it means, that this dying man looks back on his past life, reviews all the joys it could give him, and finds that the greatest joy was having read "War and Peace" and "Anna Karenina"?

Even if it was this cold and stubborn 1877. Not long after, Tolstoy life, he betrayed his life from birth to strict end, lost , he "born" female school absolute , completely devoted to theological research, translated "Gospel ". Doubtless Turgenev his method of request some sublime trick. A dying , he tells like this, is very possible to achieve the purpose, and attract Tolstoy attention. But this matter for him is very important, so he applies the weak quantity appeal his wishes! 'How should I be glad…' He is a non-believer, he knows when the loess covers his body, everything for him will be over, but he does not neglect that after he leaves the world everything ' ' will flourish to select work yesterday.

He did not act like those disgustingly fashionable things that became common later, he did not do such a thing, comparing art, poetry itself, with life, thinking it was not important enough, similar events should bring shame to the author. Truly important work should increase in the world, is

concerned, this heart will soon stop beating, in addition, Russia should help this treasure to increase, that is this cosmopolitan patriotism. 'My friend, great writer of the Russian land!'

A friend visited Socrates in his prison cell on the eve of his execution and found him learning a new tune on the seven-stringed lyre. The friend exclaimed: "Socrates, you will be executed soon, and you are still learning a new song today?" To this, Socrates replied, "Well, my friend, what time will you allow me to learn it?" This is the spirit of our letter.

But after declaring hopelessness, Turgenev pleads with another writer to exert his great talent as before, he adds a reason, an encouragement: "Because your talent comes to you from the source of all things, as you know." That event is somewhat immortal. Turgenev wrote Fathers and Sons, Smoke, A Nest of Gentlefolk, and other early works, Russia serfdom opening the way, but this insignificant sentence should not be forgotten, soaring above other works. We see this patient, at the time was to make Tolstoy understand bearing the responsibility that talent should bear, we see how he in a religious manner, conferring to this admirable post-mortem, we feel how he's suspicious, in his bravely dead and without religion, how is it for the sake of readable, unwilling to use less pseudo means, while saying things we completely neglect, the results produce this precise and transcendental turn of phrase. This great man and writer greatly tolerated another writer, he believed in religion, or at least fervently wished to believe in religion, but he himself was forever true, true like a person, true like a philosopher.

No, indeed, humanity is not an empty word. Do not be absorbed by the pretenses of this turbulent era, nor by those violent people, nor be deceived by those with Stvitus stancer and those with whatever creeds chanting! Go towards truth, towards simplicity, have a benevolent heart, remain optimistic, strive for tranquility in sorrow and hardship, love life and do not hate death, cultivate the spirit and do not be disturbed by external things – since the beginning of the world, there has been no better lesson. (Translated by Xiang Yu)

Landscape by Zi Kai Painting 202

— TK

Mr. Lu Xun and Literature 203

— Qinwen

"Giant of the literary world," "Authority of the literary world," since Mr. Lu Xun's death, these kinds of titles can almost be seen every day in magazines and newspapers. Just the book "Call to Arms" alone, in fact, with just the story of "The True Story of Ah Q," at least in terms of creation, Mr. Lu Xun had already cut a deep line between old and new literature. No matter what, in the New Literature world, it cannot be denied that he was an advanced pioneer; and few people can compare to his strength. However, he himself did not intend to be known for literature; this can be understood by simply reading the preface to "Call to Arms." The production of "Call to Arms," in his original intention, was out of necessity. Because he knew that "what is good at changing the spirit is, I... believe that of course it should be literature and art;"

He clearly stated this kind of preface in "Call to Arms." But he also understood that, in order to change the spirit of the general public, there were things more important than literature. He engaged in literature and had a grand harvest. It is said that as long as one of his short articles was published, no matter what magazine, sales would certainly increase several times. In fact, many young people had received his guidance and were influenced by him.

The reason why Mr. Lu Xun's articles were so touching and so popular was because he made various efforts besides writing articles; of course, he was able to resist the powerful and support the weak, to fight for the glory of the nation, in reality, he was a brave warrior, and literature to him was just a kind of tool like knives and guns. Although Mr. Lu Xun's means of making everyone believe often changed, the spirit of struggling desperately at the forefront of the times was always consistent, and his views on literature certainly changed along with the trend. This is not surprising. New literature, of course, must be based on actual life; Mr. Lu Xun, the "Call to Arms" that he began to create, was "literature of problems;" -- in order to change the spirit of his foolish and weak compatriots, he described it in great detail in the preface to "Call to Arms."

Mr. Lu Xun, who has been writing for thirty years, if he "stuck to" the old ways, then there would be no so-called "giant" or "authority," or "Lu Xun" as a profession.

Engaging in literature can usually be divided into four aspects to start with, which are promotion, creation, criticism, and introduction. Mr. Lu Xun promoted it more than thirty years ago, created world-famous works such as "Call to Arms," criticism can be seen everywhere in his miscellaneous essays, and introduction, his translations are also numerous enough. What is more noteworthy is the literature about the damaged and weak ethnic groups. Then he has all four aspects complete, and all are excellent. But this is not surprising, he has a long history, and it was not achieved all at once.

Mourning Lu Xun 204

— Hirabayashi Taiko

Oh, you are gone

You, the wet nurse who fed the souls of the Chinese people

Your health was our happiness (Note 1)

In the East

This sinful year

Gorky passed away

And you are gone again

The Chinese people are in suffering

The jackals are showing off their ferocity

"I am a Chinese

For the sake of the motherland

When this pen is useless

I still have my actions

As long as I live

"I should do my best for the masses" (Note 2)

Could you not suffer a little more hardship

Do a little more service

"My father did not leave me any money..."

These are your heartbreaking words in illness

Your illness was not incurable

Yet, ah

You finally left

Is what you left for people also too little

Today, the Chinese people are in suffering

The masses of the whole world are also in suffering

The pack of jackals are showing off their ferocity

Did you just peacefully close those hawk eyes

And not give them one more glare

October 20, 1936, Luozhen.

Note 1: Tian Jun's line in the "Gift in Illness" in "Writer" August issue.

Note 2: Not the complete original words of the Mr., but in answering Xu Maoyong and in the article about the anti-Japanese united front problem and in other random thoughts of the Mr., he revealed this kind of meaning.

Note 3: Tian Jun's original words of the Mr. in illness recorded in the "Gift in Illness."

The Question of the Founder of Naturalistic Drama 205

— Hou Feng

Regarding French naturalistic drama, people generally believe that it started with Henri Becque, but in reality, the one who first established the theory of naturalism and then struggled to implement this theory was Émile Zola. Because Becque's naturalistic play "Les Corbeaux" was first performed at the Comédie-Française in France in 1882; Zola published his theory of naturalistic drama in newspapers such as "Bien Public" and "Voltaire," causing heated debate in the theater world at the time, but this was in 1876-77. As for his first naturalistic play, "Thérèse Raquin," its performance was in 1873. Therefore, regarding the name of naturalistic drama, establishing the theory of naturalistic drama, practice, and struggle in various aspects, Zola was nine years earlier than Becque.

For the proposal and practice of the theory of naturalistic drama, Zola became the target of public criticism in the French literary world at the time. The opposition's slander and injury to him can be said to have been all-pervasive, and he was hit by the "non-purchase alliance" established by various theaters against his plays, but Zola did not lose heart because of this. The malicious criticism of what is called "despicable" cannot really erase the actual existence of the theoretical drama of our founder of naturalism based on the spirit of the times, but rather reveals the magnitude of his realistic power. So his "Thérèse Raquin" also achieved a "startling" effect.

Regarding the traces of the growth of naturalistic drama, we can seek it in Zola's theory and works. Starting from his "Thérèse Raquin," which was originally a novel and later rewritten into a play, he faithfully practiced his theory, whether in form or content, all starting from naturalism, all the way to the later "Renée" (five-act play, first performed on April 16, 1887), etc., all clearly expressed the process of naturalistic drama's conception, growth, and maturity. As for Becque's plays later being called models of realism, it was due to being stimulated by that kind of opportunity.

The realistic drama movement that was set off at Antoine's Théâtre Libre was entirely the expansion of Zola's theory. And those famous realistic playwrights from the end of the 19th century to around the time of World War I were directly or indirectly influenced by Zola's dramatic theory. Even now, Zola's dramatic theory is still a major trend in the theater world. This is certainly not without reason. In short, Zola is not only a guide for naturalistic drama, but also the founder of naturalistic drama.

The Man with a Tragic History 206

— TK

A Memory 207

— Yongzhi

Because a friend overseas wanted me to forward a letter to Mr. Lu Xun, I had the opportunity to meet him once. The letter was very ordinary, and I could have just given it to the Uchiyama Bookstore to forward to him, and that would have been the end of it. However, my friend specifically instructed me to hand it over in person and had something he wanted to discuss with him face to face, so I had no choice but to go find him and meet him.

That day, I walked to Uchiyama Bookstore bathed in the gentle sunlight. I explained my purpose, and Mr. Uchiyama asked me to wait while he notified him on my behalf. I sat and waited for a while, but unexpectedly, a lady came. After Mr. Uchiyama's explanation, I learned that she was sent by Mr. Lu Xun.

"I am Mr. Zhou's student," she introduced herself first, "Mr. Zhou is not at home. If there is anything, we might as well talk about it first." She said very gently.

"This is a letter from Mr. ×, you can take a look," I said as I took a letter from my pocket and handed it to the lady. After she read it, knowing that Mr. × instructed that we had something to discuss face to face and that the letter also had to be handed over in person, she returned the letter to me as before. She also arranged the time and place for our meeting the next day on his behalf. The next day I went to Uchiyama Bookstore, and Mr. Lu Xun had already arrived. He was sitting diagonally near the door, his face was very gray and pale, his clothes were not very clean, but his eyes looked at me very powerfully. Of course, after Mr. Uchiyama explained, we began to talk.

I handed him the letter from Mr. ×.

"The person you met yesterday is my wife. She told you that she was my student, right?" he said with a slight smile, as if he was making a clarification while reading the letter.

"Haha," I only responded like this. "That is Ms. Guangping from your correspondence books, right?" I thought about saying this, but I only smiled and did not say it out loud. He immediately stood up.

"Let's go to the café in front to talk in detail, shall we?" He looked at me, I only nodded, and then I walked out of Uchiyama Bookstore with him.

We walked to a small café about half a mile away from Uchiyama Bookstore. After we were seated, he continued reading the letter. After reading the letter, he said to me very happily:

"What do you think of my health? They are always worried about my health. Actually, they have been abroad for too long and are used to seeing huge Westerners, so naturally they think my body is weak. In the end, I don't have any illness. It seems that I am not strong, but in reality, I am still okay. I am working every day." He said faintly, dragging out his not-so-fluent Mandarin with some Shaoxing accent mixed in.

"I hope that you can go abroad to recuperate for a while as your friends expect," I replied to him without thinking. In reality, I really felt sorry for this old warrior. His body was not doing well, and the environment was oppressively cruel to him. How could he support himself with such internal and external attacks? "And Mr. × is afraid that you are having economic difficulties. He has also entrusted a friend to help you borrow money, which will be returned after you arrive there, and this friend has already agreed." I continued, saying that my friend wanted me to speak plainly to him, fearing that he would be troubled by economics. But I did not answer him about his health. Because I saw that he had quite strong confidence in his own health, but in reality, his body was not doing well, so how could I answer? By the way, I also told him that his friends overseas had heard many unfavorable rumors about him. Everyone was worried, so they hoped even more that he would go abroad to live for a while.

He smiled, smoked a cigarette, and said slowly:

"Rumors, well, there are rumors all year round, how can there be so many that stand out? Going abroad to live for a while is naturally good, and I have also planned to do so. But if I were to be scared away by rumors, then there is no need. Because it is impossible to live abroad for a long time, and I will have to come back to China eventually. At that time, there may be even more rumors." After he said these words, he suddenly asked me if I knew Mr. ××. I told him that I had known him for ten years and that I was also his teacher at ×× University.

He heard that I knew Mr. Xu. So he told me a lot of news about Mr. Xu, from Mr. Xu's recent life, to the course of his death. As well as many rumors about him after his death. He also told me that he was collecting various posthumous works for him. He planned to spend half a year compiling Mr. Xu's posthumous works. And tidy up all his own things, and then talk about going abroad. Not being able to go abroad immediately, this is also an important reason.

"His posthumous works are really valuable, they will give great contributions to mankind, I am editing his posthumous works, not only for the private feelings of friends." He said this in a slightly sad tone at the end.

I was silent for a while and asked him if he was planning to write a reply to Mr. ×. He thought for a moment and said, "No need, please tell them on my behalf."

Finally, we agreed on the place for correspondence and meeting. Because I had asked him that in the future, if there was a place where I needed his help in writing.

We walked out of the café together, nodded to each other lightly, and then walked away in opposite directions. I walked about five yards away and looked back at him. He was slowly walking diagonally into the northwest corner, bathed in the sunlight.

After separating, there was no second chance to meet. Later, in the newspaper, I found the news of the old warrior's death, which gave me a severe shock! I couldn't breathe for half a day. In the past few days, I have only been looking for news about his death in the newspaper. After all, the spirit of our old warrior who fought for national liberation has been distributed to the broad masses! In recent days, thousands upon thousands of workers, students, and shop assistants are vying to pay their respects to the remains of our dead old warrior. Doesn't this show that his unfinished cause has been inherited by these successors?

Straw Toffee 208

— Chen Zizhan

"How annoying, the candy maker is here again. Last time my little brother ate his candy Buddha and had diarrhea for several days. He's here again!"

Jumping out of the rickshaw with Jingyi, I saw a crowd of children surrounding a candy maker at the entrance of the alley. The candy maker was blowing sugar into the shape of a sugar rat and pinching its ears and tail with his hands. Jingyi found our little brother in the crowd of children, and couldn't help but feel a little impatient.

"Don't look down on the candy maker. Although he makes a living on the street, he is an art master."

Jingyi couldn't help laughing when she heard what I said. She said, "Where are there so many art masters?"

I thought, there are many art masters on the street, such as the calligrapher who draws turtles on the walls, the musician who sells huqins and flutes, the playwright who plays wooden puppets, the genius poet who sings lotus ballads, the literary failures who narrate or confess in their complaints, as well as the sculptors who knead gray dough figures or make clay figurines, the national art doctors who sell magic tricks, and the great directors who turn peep shows. Although they have never openly claimed to be art masters, it is not too much to call them that, is it?

I saw that on the candy maker's stall, a clump of grass was inserted with many artworks for people to exhibit without charging admission. Those were all goods he wanted to clear out, not for sale and not priced high. However, the grass clump seemed to be divided into two distinct layers: the lower layer consisted of monkeys, cats, rats, chickens, dogs, fish, shrimp, spoons, and still life objects such as trumpets and water pipes; the upper layer consisted of human figures, from Guan Gong holding a broadsword to generals wearing command swords, as if symbolizing heroes who dared to fight in ancient and modern times. Could it be that the slogan of "national defense" has also influenced this art master? I wonder if they have ever had debates over the slogans of "national defense" and "nation"? However, what I paid attention to was not here, but just staring blankly at those sugar-made heroes wearing armor and carrying weapons. Although they are sugar-made heroes, they may not be able to defend against insults and fight wars, but they are also awe-inspiring and inviolable, as if suppressing a group of pitiful animals in their lower layer.

"Dad, Mom is waiting for you to go back for dinner."

I heard my little brother calling me, and then I left the candy stall. But from this sugar-made hero, I thought of "straw toffee" - a story in history. It turns out that the art of kneading sugar figures has "existed since ancient times."

During the Sui Dynasty, there was an upright official named Liang Yanguang, who, after losing his official position, lived in seclusion at home. One day, the emperor summoned him to ask questions and ordered him to be the prefect of Zhao Prefecture. He said, "I won't go to Zhao Prefecture. If I go, I'll go to Xiang Prefecture." The emperor said, "Haven't you been to Xiang Prefecture before?" He said, "Last time I was the prefect of Xiang Prefecture, I didn't want to disturb the people, so I didn't want to do too much, thinking that it was better to be still than to move. Unexpectedly, the people there laughed at me for being confused and bullied me for being weak, comparing me to a sugar-made official, thinking that I was good-looking but useless, and giving me the nickname 'straw toffee.' Therefore, I lost my official position. I thought I would never come out again in my life, but unexpectedly, the emperor's grace allowed me to be the prefect of Zhao Prefecture again. So, I still want to return to Xiang Prefecture to do something and wash away my previous shame." The emperor then allowed him. This time, when he went to Xiang Prefecture, he actually became a very capable official. The Book of Sui includes this story, I wonder if it is reliable?

"Straw toffee" and "sugar-made heroes" also look like people, arousing wonderful thoughts that people are also like them. The candy maker is worthy of being an art master.

Japanese Preparation for Negotiations 220

— I

According to recent telegraph dispatches, how to break through the deadlock in Sino-Japanese negotiations is attracting attention from all parties. However, it is currently believed that the parties are still in the meeting and consultation stage. As generally observed, the Japanese side is now gathering a large number of key members to discuss the tactics for conducting the negotiations. We are not diplomats by nature, so we naturally do not understand what is meant by diplomatic tactics, let alone the methods of diplomatic tactics. However, what we do know is that since Ambassador Kawagoe arrived in Beijing to negotiate the adjustment of Sino-Japanese relations with our country's authorities, we have only seen one negotiation that failed to reach a consensus, and then Kuwashima came to China with new instructions from the Japanese side. Then, we saw a second negotiation that still failed to reach a consensus, so Suma returned to his country, also bringing so-called new instructions. But what are these two sets of new instructions? What is the situation of their negotiations? To what extent have they negotiated, and how? We are still lost in a fog, completely baffled.

We only know that the Japanese side has two original diplomatic policies: one is "dual diplomacy" and the other is "diplomatic unification." The so-called "dual diplomacy" and "diplomatic unification" are nothing more than a combination of soft and hard tactics, a simultaneous application of firmness and flexibility. In plain language, it is simply a fist and a candy, a combination of kindness and power. Looking at the current diplomatic situation of the Japanese side, it is truly strange. On the one hand, they send Kawagoe to Beijing to conduct "consultative" negotiations with our country's authorities, while on the other hand, alarming news is coming from the north every day. One report says that rioters took advantage of Japanese military exercises to attempt to cause trouble, so Tianjin is under special martial law. Another report says that the Japanese side conducted a large-scale exercise for a week in the Ping-Lu area, with a large number of Japanese soldiers marching through the city of Ping. Another report says that the Japanese side arbitrarily dispatched police and set up posts in the Ping-Jin area. Another report says that a certain party is actively invading westward, and Suiyuan is in imminent danger. Is this Sino-Japanese negotiation ultimately intended to proceed in a peaceful negotiation manner? Or is it intended to proceed in a reckless manner without peace? Assuming that it is intended to proceed in a peaceful negotiation manner, then while the two sides are negotiating and have not yet reached a breaking point, there should not be any arbitrary reckless actions in the Ping-Jin area. Assuming that it is intended to proceed in a reckless manner without peace, then the two sides do not need to engage in any more consultative negotiations. Any diplomat or non-diplomat can understand this basic common sense.

Therefore, our diplomacy, relying solely on consultative negotiations, is still not enough. We should also use dual diplomatic tactics like the Japanese. Because they use dual diplomatic tactics, we should also use dual diplomatic tactics to be correct. Otherwise, diplomatic negotiations will continue to drag on day after day, while the situation in North China will become more and more tense day after day. In the end, we will still have to say that it is an accomplished fact, and any rejection or denial on our part will be a belated effort. Is this situation a good approach to diplomatic tactics? Furthermore, a certain Japanese news agency stated the other day that the general public is quite resentful of the delay in Sino-Japanese negotiations. It is not known whether this statement is ironic. However, looking at the current situation, delay can also be said to be a type of diplomatic tactic. Therefore, the authorities must pay serious attention to this point and not neglect it.

— Li Xuelian

There, the lanterns are on, the faces painted with somewhat frightening white and red mixtures, crying mournfully as they struggle to shout for customers.

"Times are bad, luck is bad, even walking is going backwards! Alas—" A woman who is only twenty-five or six years old is already complaining about fate and the cruel time that has aged her. The melancholic sigh soured the "young chick" who had just come out of the coop standing next to her. (Note 1)

"Sister Aying, I think, if mother agrees, moving to the newly reclaimed land might be a little better for business…"

"Moving is not that easy! Would mother still invest in me? In the newly reclaimed land, someone my age really can't stand it!…"

They stared with stagnant eyes, greedily eyeing the fully loaded customers brought from the station, as if not moved by their chicken-like shouts. They jealously and attentively watched these vehicles, one long string after another, pulling west, pulling towards the newly reclaimed land, Xidi, Huangsha, and gone.

This section of the ten-mile-long embankment, with the Haizhu Iron Bridge forming a very distinct boundary line, the lively night market west of the bridge is giving the aging Dongdi a very vicious satire. The night market on this side is also two worlds. On the north side are large buildings. In addition to the two towering foreign buildings of the Sincere Company and the Sun Sun Company, all kinds of lively taverns, movie theaters, Cantonese opera theaters, and various styles are all available. The electric lights and neon lights are intensely hurting people's eyes. People? Whether gentlemen in well-tailored suits, ladies on the list of suppression (Note 2), or people of middle class and above, are all crowded into a long line, like fish on a skewer, never ceasing. At this time, it is already the active time of the night.

On the sea side, that is another night world.

The embankment that has been planned for quite some time has been completed by seven or eight tenths. Many foreign buildings have also been built, but it seems that some open space must be left to develop this night world, so that this place called the newly reclaimed land can accommodate the gathering of the nine sects and three streams.

Here, the light of kerosene lamps and Meifu lamps reflects a mysterious world. Here, there are many temporary stalls: there are "philosophers" who have been driven out of the City God Temple, scholars, and book stalls specializing in "little books" and erotic pictures. There are fish porridge stalls that have moved a broken boat to be a living sign. There are herbal tea stalls that knock on tortoise shells and shout loudly. There are brave warriors who sell martial arts in the arena, and there are also magicians who perform magic tricks. There are treasures selling "thunder-struck medicine." There are also storytellers who are good at attracting people… In this way, people are connected in a series, shuttling back and forth.

On the edge of the embankment, outside is the Pearl River of "Pearl River Night Moon."

Page 18

The flower boats moored by the shore are chained together as if they were doing exercises. Some boat heads have one or two boat prostitutes standing in their underwear: some are covered with curtains, and the mysterious lights and sensational laughter fluctuate, causing the boats to move. Three or five people with their eyes squinted into a line are tiptoeing there, their hearts pounding. In the dark places, groups of women, with high-pitched voices, call out as if they are嬌滴滴：

"Call a boat, hey! Take a river tour! Call a prostitute for the night!…"

(Note 1) A prostitute who has not been doing business for long. (Note 2) There was once a prevailing trend of suppressing strange costumes here, but later it was taken but not suppressed.

Fishing Tax 224

— Zhi Fu

——Old History Newly Compiled—— The sun in June hung high in the sky, its rays shining like raging fire, scorching the fields, the river… The whole earth was simply like an iron pot on fire.

Heaven had sent down a little rain ten days ago, but until now, not a single drop had fallen again. The sky was clear and bright, with not a single cloud in sight.

The rice in the fields had all withered from the scorching, and the water in the river channel was about to dry up. The small ponds had long faced the sky, with many dried dead fish and shrimp stuck to the edges, emitting bursts of fishy stench under the sunlight.…………

The fishing boats at Sanjiang Estuary were now stranded on the shallow shore one by one. The fishermen had no fish to catch and had stopped working.

"This murderous year! If it doesn't rain again and the fierce drought presses down on the world, good heavens! Then we poor people will be in big trouble!…"

The fishermen pointed to the sky and gestured on the ground, clamoring amidst tears and wails. Even the sixty-year-old man, Xiao En, kept looking at the clear blue sky, roaring and complaining.

It had been half a full month since there had been any rain.

But in these past two weeks, the Ding family had not relaxed their fishing tax on the fishermen because of the drought. They had sent the old servant Wu Min along with three or four strong men to the river to urge them to pay.

"…You bunch of dogs! Who dares not pay the fishing tax? Does anyone dare to boldly resist the Ding family's rules?… Who is leading the way! Hey, damn fellows!…"

The old servant Wu, relying on the power of the Ding family, wore an iron-blue face everywhere, raised his sparse whiskers, his eyes as big as wine glasses, grumbling with anger and curses as he came to Xiao En's boat.

Xiao En was sitting silently on the boat. At this moment, he stood up and pointed to the dry river channel, saying to him:

"Sir, please take a look! This kind of river channel… Where can we fishermen find a living!… The small fish are all dead, and the big ones have long swam into the big river. Fishing tax, we are not resisting the Ding family's rules, but really… really we have no way to think!…"

"No way to think? Are you Xiao the old head setting it up?" Old servant Wu turned his head to look at Xiao En, his eyes bathing in blood. "Sir! The facts are in front of us, it's not just me, Xiao, who is advocating this… This time, I trouble you to report back to your family's master, and wait for us to pay the tax next year. If the year is better next year, we will add interest, that would be good!…" Xiao En was very energetic, with a face full of smiles as he greeted him, rolling a lot of words from his dry lips under his two white beards, begging Wu old servant bitterly.

"Bah! Bold fellows!… Don't dawdle, first take you old dog to the Ding family to await disposal…"

Saying that: Wu old servant darted forward and grabbed Xiao En, and then the few men behind him also crowded up together.

But Xiao En was really angry. He calmed down and waved his two powerful fists to resist.

The shouting was as noisy as a collapsing wall. However, without him taking action, the strong men fell to the ground one by one like scallions and garlic, and Wu old servant was trampled under his feet.

Xiao daughter Guan Ying was in the back of the cabin. Hearing the sound on the shore, she hurriedly climbed out of the cabin, went ashore to stop her father's fists and feet, and pulled Wu old servant up from under her feet with one hand. But the few men who had been knocked down were now dazed, panting heavily…

"It's turned upside down! Xiao old dog has turned upside down!… Okay, go back and tell the master, tomorrow come and arrest you for disposition in court…"

Wu old servant held his own head, saying while beckoning to the group of defeated crickets-like men, all scurrying into the cracked fields.

Xiao En wiped the dust on his clothes, looking at the backs of their group, emitting a burst of indifferent ridicule…

The next day, at noon, the sun was still hanging high in the sky, just like yesterday. The fishermen along the dry river channel at Sanjiang Estuary all heard the news and gathered.

They all seemed to have forgotten that it was hot weather, exposing their bare bodies to the scorching sun, listening to Xiao En standing on the bow of the boat and saying loudly:

"Uh! We don't want to pay fishing tax anymore! Whoever pays is a traitor to us all!…" He said energetically, while raising his clenched fist, pretending to be full of remaining anger.

"Uncle Suo's words are right!"

"…That's right! We all have to act accordingly!"

The fishermen also clenched their fists, raising their dark arms that had been exposed to the sun like tree bark, expressing great sympathy and support…

Guan Ying leaned beside her father, wanting to speak several times, but she was a little shy, and still timidly lowered her head and fiddled with her clothes.

This time - she really couldn't bear the anger in her heart, and finally rushed to say:

"…Things have come to this point, we must make a decision!… You think, this is a public river channel, why should we fishermen use our sweat and blood to pay respects to the Ding family. We were stupid before!… Taking advantage of everyone being united, let's abolish this harsh tax… " After she finished speaking, a layer of bright red blush could not help but appear on her cheeks…

At this time, everyone's hearts had firmly embraced a great will.

Mei Luo Xiang

Mei Luo Xiang finally could not resist the temptation of material things. After not having a play to perform in Shanghai for six months, she was provoked by her fellow actress Xiao Chunlan's words, and she still threw herself into Bai Senqing's control.

She lived with Bai Senqing for two months and gradually became a little bored. Suddenly, she received a telegram from Ma Ziying, who had made a fortune in Gulangyu, Xiamen, saying that he would immediately come to Shanghai to fulfill their alliance. This left Mei Luo Xiang stunned.

Opening Chapter "Shen Fengxi is Humiliated" Disappointed, old lovers speak of Ruan Liu. Unexpectedly, the husband seeks a title. Asking one's heart, it is difficult to speak. I think of you, there are many beautiful women in the world. They are all gently playing the zither and drum. Not like me, a bitter plum by the roadside for people to pluck. I am left to face the wind and rain. Only the county magistrate said, forgive me. Accompanying you to Hangzhou. However, the general's power is boundless. How can I leave without saying goodbye. Even if I can hide for a while. I am afraid that it will be difficult to escape to the ends of the earth. Therefore, I found it difficult to answer for a while. I did not realize that my face was blushing with red. I took out a check to repay you. Doubling the amount for you. Who knew that he tore them into pieces like butterflies. Flying up to the clouds and not leaving. Therefore, I went home in a洋卓, with worries in my heart.

Opening Chapter "Gong Shu"

The Western Palace is quiet at night with the fragrance of a hundred flowers. Wanting to roll up the bead curtain, the spring hate is long. The favorite concubine sits alone on the agarwood couch. Heaven on Earth

Spring has returned. Spring has returned. People hear flowers blooming everywhere. Those who plant flowers are content. Those who love flowers cherish memories. Those who sell flowers earn money. Those who admire flowers gain pleasure. Famous flowers and fragrant herbs. Naturally, people will plant them. The spring breeze blows across the fields, allowing these natural beauties to share the love of the world. Green mountains and apricot blossoms.碧clear waters surging. Light clouds and a high sky. The moon is round and the flowers are beautiful. The serene and secluded immortal island. Hard to paint, hard to describe. Moon and flowers in the morning. Every night is a beautiful night. Everyone laughs. Everywhere, carefree. The spring scenery of Heaven on Earth never ages. Feasts are laid out. Singing and dancing surround. Fine wine and delicious food. Inevitably, a lively scene. Silver candles burn high. Sandalwood smoke drifts. The immortal officials arrange everything meticulously. With wine and food, we are all drunk and full. With poetry and classics, we discuss and refine together. We wish for those with secret sorrows to be blessed. Jade faces remain charming. Rosy cheeks remain youthful. Green mountains remain, and the water flows forever. Eternal youth. How much true affection and true love is there? Difficult to achieve, difficult to endure, hatred difficult to dispel. We wish for lovers to be blessed. May all wishes be fulfilled. May there be no ill-fated encounters. No worries, no anxieties. Always joyful.

Movies

Two New Domestic Films Released 230

Mingxing - "Night Meeting" Yihua - "Map of Treasures"

"Night Meeting," a blockbuster directed by Li Pingqian of Mingxing Film Company, depicts a tragic and sensational murder case that occurred in a nocturnal city. It is lively, dynamic, and presented with the latest style. Starring Gu Lanjun, Huang Naishuang, Gong Jianong, and newcomer Xie Jun, it officially premieres today at the Jincheng Grand Theater. Before the film, there will also be a newsreel of the death of the great literary figure Lu Xun, featuring Lu Xun's residence, family, his library during his lifetime, and the events of the funeral day, including the final respects from tens of thousands of people and the iron ranks. In addition, Mingxing Company is offering viewers a "Mingxing Friendship Postcard" as a special bonus.

Yihua's detective blockbuster "Map of Treasures" is a masterpiece following "The Bloodbath of Newlyweds." The director Yue Feng's techniques and the actors' skilled performances will surely leave a deep impression on the audience. It premieres today at the Xingguang Karkua Theater. Both theaters are offering half-price discounts to Boy Scouts who wear their uniforms or badges. This is an opportunity not to be missed.

Colorful Literary Film "Ramona" 231

Premieres Today at the Grand Cathay

The long-awaited colorful literary blockbuster "Ramona" premieres today at the Grand Cathay. The film tells the story of a young woman, Ramona, of mixed race. Although a white man is in love with her, his mother opposes the marriage, making it impossible. Ramona soon marries an Indian with a sense of responsibility and goes with him to the Indian settlement, where they farm and live. The following year, they have a daughter and are very happy. Unfortunately, their land is suddenly confiscated by the American government. They have no power to resist, so they have to go to the mountains to find another way to make a living. Later, due to wind and rain, the child falls ill and they take shelter in the home of a white woman. Ramona's husband rides to town to hire a doctor, but instead of finding a doctor, he is killed for riding a white man's horse. Ramona becomes a homeless woman. The white man who loved her before hears the news and comes to find her. When they meet, she looks back on the past and cannot help but burst into tears, falling into his arms. With Loretta Young's graceful and charming demeanor, she is of course very suitable for the role of Ramona. The other supporting actors also give strong performances. The film's color is also exquisite, bringing the beautiful scenery and bright sunshine of California to the screen, captivating the audience.
